	document.body.style.overflow = "hidden";
	
	window.addEventListener("load", () => {
		setTimeout(() => {
			const preloader = document.getElementById("preloader");
			
			if (preloader) {
				// Add fade out transition
				preloader.style.transition = "opacity 0.5s ease";
				preloader.style.opacity = "0";

					preloader.remove();

			}
		}, 5000);

			<script src="https://ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/jquery/3.7.1/jquery.min.js"></script><link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/nanogallery2@3/dist/css/nanogallery2.min.css" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css"><script type="text/javascript" src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/nanogallery2@3/dist/jquery.nanogallery2.min.js"></script><div id="gallery" style="width: 320px; overflow: visible;" data-nanogallery2="{

		<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-a10e222 e-grid e-con-full e-con e-child" data-id="a10e222" data-element_type="container">
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-339b5ac elementor-widget elementor-widget-music-and-video" data-id="339b5ac" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="music-and-video.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
			
		
					<div id="youtube-music-container" style="position:fixed; opacity: 0; z-index:-1;">
				<iframe id="youtube-music-player" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share" referrerpolicy="strict-origin-when-cross-origin" title="Jake Miller - Lucky Me (The proposal)" width="20" height="20" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/XysLGnlSjE0?autoplay=0&amp;loop=1&amp;playsinline=1&amp;playlist=XysLGnlSjE0&amp;enablejsapi=1&amp;origin=https%3A%2F%2Fhansen-kezia-demo.envelope.id&amp;widgetid=1&amp;forigin=https%3A%2F%2Fhansen-kezia-demo.envelope.id%2F%3Fmode%3Ddemo&amp;aoriginsup=1&amp;gporigin=https%3A%2F%2Fenvelope.id%2F&amp;vf=1"></iframe>
			</div>
		
					
		
		
		<script>
			var mp3Player;
			var ytMusicPlayer;
			var ytVideoPlayer;
			var mp3Url = "";
			var musicYoutubeUrl = "https://youtu.be/XysLGnlSjE0?si=kWZEscfXjegoN_oy";
			var videoYoutubeUrl = "";
			var isMusicReady = false;
			var isMusicPlaying = false;
			var usingMp3 = false;

			const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);

			$("#youtube-video-container").hide();

			// Initialize MP3 player if URL is provided
			if (mp3Url) {
				mp3Player = document.getElementById('mp3-player');
				usingMp3 = true;
				isMusicReady = true;
			}

			function onYouTubeIframeAPIReady() {
				if (params.get('mode') == "preview") {
					return;
				}

				musicVideoID = extractVideoID(musicYoutubeUrl);
				videoVideoID = extractVideoID(videoYoutubeUrl);

				if (musicVideoID != "" && !usingMp3) {
					ytMusicPlayer = new YT.Player('youtube-music-player', {
						height: '20',
						width: '20',
						videoId: extractVideoID(musicYoutubeUrl),
						playerVars: {
							autoplay: 0,
							loop: 1,
							playsinline: 1,
							playlist: extractVideoID(musicYoutubeUrl)
						},
						events: {
							'onReady': onMusicPlayerReady
						}
					});
				}

				if (videoVideoID != "") {
					$("#youtube-video-container").show();

					ytVideoPlayer = new YT.Player('youtube-video-player', {
						height: '360',
						width: '640',
						videoId: extractVideoID(videoYoutubeUrl),
						playerVars: {
							autoplay: 0,
							playsinline: 1,
						},
						events: {
							'onStateChange': onVideoPlayerStateChange
						}
					});
				}
			}

			function onMusicPlayerReady(event) {
				isMusicReady = true;
			}

			function onVideoPlayerStateChange(event) {
				if (params.get('mode') == "preview") {
					return;
				}

				if (event.data == YT.PlayerState.PLAYING) {
					if (usingMp3) {
						mp3Player.pause();
					} else {
						ytMusicPlayer.pauseVideo();
					}
					isMusicPlaying = false;
					$("#music-button").addClass("paused")
				} else if (event.data == YT.PlayerState.PAUSED || event.data == YT.PlayerState.ENDED) {
					if (usingMp3) {
						mp3Player.play();
					} else {
						ytMusicPlayer.playVideo();
					}
					isMusicPlaying = true;
					$("#music-button").removeClass("paused")
				}
			}

			function extractVideoID(url) {
				var regExp = /^.*((youtu.be\/)|(v\/)|(\/u\/\w\/)|(embed\/)|(watch\?))\??v?=?([^#\&\?]*).*/;
				var match = url.match(regExp);
				if (match && match[7].length == 11) {
					return match[7];
				} else {
					return "";
				}
			}

			$("#bukadisini").on("click touch", function () {
				if (params.get('mode') == "preview") {
					return;
				}

				playMusic();
			})

			$("#desktopcoverbutton").on("click touch", function () {
				if (params.get('mode') == "preview") {
					return;
				}

				playMusic();
			})

			$("#mobilecoverbutton").on("click touch", function () {
				if (params.get('mode') == "preview") {
					return;
				}

				playMusic();
			})

			$("#music-button").on("click touch", function () {
				if (params.get('mode') == "preview") {
					return;
				}

				toggleMusic();
			})

			function playMusic() {
				if (usingMp3) {
					if (!mp3Url) {
						return;
					}
					$("#music-button").show();
					mp3Player.play();
					isMusicPlaying = true;
					$("#music-button").removeClass("paused");
				} else {
					if (musicYoutubeUrl == "" || extractVideoID(musicYoutubeUrl) == "") {
						return;
					}

					$("#music-button").show();
					var playMusicInterval = setInterval(function () {
						if (isMusicReady) {
							var playerState = ytMusicPlayer.getPlayerState();
							if (playerState == 1) {
								clearInterval(playMusicInterval);
								$("#music-button").removeClass("paused")
							} else if (playerState == -1) {
								reloadMusicPlayer();
							} else {
								ytMusicPlayer.playVideo();
								isMusicPlaying = true;
							}
						}
					}, 200);
				}
			}

			function playMusicV2() {
				if (usingMp3) {
					if (!mp3Url) {
						return;
					}
					$("#music-button").show();
					mp3Player.play();
					isMusicPlaying = true;
					$("#music-button").removeClass("paused");
				} else {
					if (!musicYoutubeUrl || !extractVideoID(musicYoutubeUrl)) {
						return;
					}

					$("#music-button").show();

					// Single attempt to play
					const attemptPlay = () => {
						if (!isMusicReady) return false;

						const playerState = ytMusicPlayer.getPlayerState();
						if (playerState === 1) {
							$("#music-button").removeClass("paused");
							return true;
						} else if (playerState === -1) {
							reloadMusicPlayer();
							return false;
						} else {
							ytMusicPlayer.playVideo();
							isMusicPlaying = true;
							return false;
						}
					};

					// If first attempt fails, set up interval
					if (!attemptPlay()) {
						const playMusicInterval = setInterval(() => {
							if (attemptPlay()) {
								clearInterval(playMusicInterval);
							}
						}, 200);
					}
				}
			}

			function toggleMusic() {
				if (usingMp3) {
					if (mp3Player.paused) {
						mp3Player.play();
						isMusicPlaying = true;
						$("#music-button").removeClass("paused");
					} else {
						mp3Player.pause();
						isMusicPlaying = false;
						$("#music-button").addClass("paused");
					}
				} else {
					if (ytMusicPlayer.getPlayerState() == 1 || ytMusicPlayer.getPlayerState() == 3) {
						ytMusicPlayer.pauseVideo();
						isMusicPlaying = false;
						$("#music-button").addClass("paused")
					} else {
						ytMusicPlayer.playVideo();
						isMusicPlaying = true;
						$("#music-button").removeClass("paused")
					}
				}
			}

			function reloadMusicPlayer() {
				ytMusicPlayer.loadVideoById(extractVideoID(musicYoutubeUrl));
			}

			document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', function() {
				if (params.get('mode') == "preview") {
					return;
				}

				if (!isMusicReady) {
					return;
				}

				if (document.hidden) {
					if (usingMp3) {
						mp3Player.pause();
					} else {
						if (ytMusicPlayer) {
							ytMusicPlayer.pauseVideo();
						}
					}
					$("#music-button").addClass("paused");
				} else {
					if (isMusicPlaying) {
						if (usingMp3) {
							mp3Player.play();
						} else {
							if (ytMusicPlayer) {
								ytMusicPlayer.playVideo();
							}
						}
						$("#music-button").removeClass("paused");
					}
				}
			});

			$(document).ready(function () {
				// Load YouTube API if using YouTube for music or video
				if (!usingMp3 || videoYoutubeUrl) {
					var existingScript = $('script[src="https://www.youtube.com/iframe_api"]');
					if (existingScript.length > 0) {
						existingScript.remove();
					}

					var s = document.createElement("script");
					s.type = "text/javascript";
					s.src = "https://www.youtube.com/iframe_api";
					$("head").append(s);
				}
			});
		</script>
				</div>
				</div>
				</div>
				</div>

			<script>
  ((w, d) => {
    let targetElementCollection;
    const targetElementSelector = ".reanimate";
    const inViewClass = "in-view";
    const defaultTop = "-10px";
    const defaultBottom = "-10px";

    d.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
      init();
    });

    const init = () => {
      targetElementCollection = d.querySelectorAll(targetElementSelector);
      targetElementCollection.forEach((el) => {
        initElement(el);
      });
    };

    const initElement = (element) => {
      const top = element.dataset.ioTop ? element.dataset.ioTop : defaultTop;
      const bottom = element.dataset.ioBottom
        ? element.dataset.ioBottom
        : defaultBottom;
      const rootMargin = top + " 0px " + bottom + " 0px ";

      let options = {
        root: null,
        rootMargin: rootMargin,
        threshold: 0.01,
      };

      let observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries, observer) => {
        entries.forEach((entry) => {
          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
            element.classList.add(inViewClass);
          } else {
            element.classList.remove(inViewClass);
          }
        });
      }, options);

      observer.observe(element);
    };
  })(window, document);
</script>

<script>
    const reanimateElements = document.querySelectorAll('.replay');

    const observer1 = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        entries.forEach((entry) => {
            const element = entry.target;
            
            if (entry.isIntersecting && element.shouldReanimate) {
                element.style.visibility = 'visible';
                const originalClasses = element.className;
    
                element.className = ''; 
                void element.offsetWidth; 
                element.className = originalClasses; 
                element.shouldReanimate = false;
            }
        });
    }, {
        threshold: 0.8
    });
    
    const observer2 = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        entries.forEach((entry) => {
            const element = entry.target;
            
            if (!entry.isIntersecting) {
                element.style.visibility = 'hidden';
                element.shouldReanimate = true;
            }
        });
    });

    reanimateElements.forEach((el) => {
        observer1.observe(el);
        observer2.observe(el);
    });
</script>		</div>

					<script type="text/javascript">
				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
			</script>
			<script id="wp-block-template-skip-link-js-after">
	( function() {
		var skipLinkTarget = document.querySelector( 'main' ),
			sibling,
			skipLinkTargetID,
			skipLink;

		// Early exit if a skip-link target can't be located.
		if ( ! skipLinkTarget ) {
			return;
		}

		/*
		 * Get the site wrapper.
		 * The skip-link will be injected in the beginning of it.
		 */
		sibling = document.querySelector( '.wp-site-blocks' );

		// Early exit if the root element was not found.
		if ( ! sibling ) {
			return;
		}

		// Get the skip-link target's ID, and generate one if it doesn't exist.
		skipLinkTargetID = skipLinkTarget.id;
		if ( ! skipLinkTargetID ) {
			skipLinkTargetID = 'wp--skip-link--target';
			skipLinkTarget.id = skipLinkTargetID;
		}

		// Create the skip link.
		skipLink = document.createElement( 'a' );
		skipLink.classList.add( 'skip-link', 'screen-reader-text' );
		skipLink.href = '#' + skipLinkTargetID;
		skipLink.innerHTML = 'Skip to content';

		// Inject the skip link.
		sibling.parentElement.insertBefore( skipLink, sibling );
	}() );
	
</script>
